msg:Severe rain made the K train delayed. Decided 1 night in Guangzhou with a new ticket back to Shenzhen. 

The rooms here are good. Refreshing beer at mini-bar. Goo bathroom facilities. Relaxed and got ready to set out for some appetizer, dinner, and music. Rain was off and on. HOWEVER, 

Never got to leave. The Sashimi was within 30 minutes unable to finish. Despite the portion well worth the value, I was ill from the fish. Right away informed lobby lounge bar, and informed him I had to go rest. I was sick. Slept today 5am. Front desk got water from housekeeping. Luckily had electrolytes in luggage. 

By checkout, front desk had already informed manager, so requested food portion for refund through WeChat. Despite not leaving the hotel, the staff and comfort of room helped. Still very ill, but was able to make it to the train. Will get sashimi at sushi/sashimi restaurants from now on. Hoping the bacteria does not lead to infection.

msg:After traveling for many years, this Marriott hotel in Guangzhou is really not flattering:
üöó Transportation:
Upstairs in Zhengjia, the surrounding area is very congested during holidays, but shopping malls and other places are still very convenient.

üßπHygiene:
Hygiene is generally okay, especially during the epidemic, hygiene is indeed a bit stricter than usual.

üçÉEnvironment and services:
This mainly talks about facilities. 1. The parking lot and Zhengjia are shared. I called the hotel before booking and the hotel replied that parking is free and can be parked in area b5-6. I asked people everywhere in the parking lot, and finally found area b5. There were no parking spaces, only a few dedicated parking spaces, so I called again to see if the dedicated parking spaces could be opened. The hotel replied that there are no dedicated parking spaces. You can park on the first and second floor, as long as there is a space. I was confused on the spot. If it was negative one or two, I could stop casually. I should have informed him clearly on the first call. I couldn‚Äôt even explain the matter clearly on the phone. 2. The design of the hotel elevator is also speechless. You can go from the first floor to the lobby on the fifth floor. In the lobby, you have to transfer to the elevator to go to the room. Services such as luggage are all on the first floor. Compared with driving up from the first floor by car, you don‚Äôt know at all. What services are there on the first floor? Moreover, due to the epidemic, food delivery is not allowed. If you want to go to the first floor, you must go to the fifth floor first, and then transfer to the elevator to get to the first floor. Because there are only two elevators to the first floor. If you are unlucky, you can only go to the first floor first and then transfer. Minus one. 3. The ceiling of the floor is relatively low and depressing, and there are no obvious signs around it. When you get out of the room and go to the elevator, you can't find the direction at all. You can only rely on your own impressions. 4. What‚Äôs even more strange is that there is no USB port for charging in the room. When I called the guest room, the room only sent one charging port. Compared to us who have four mobile phones and two iPads, we have to take turns charging them all night. This kind of hardware facilities is speechless. Moreover, there is no mineral water or paper towels in the room. These necessary supplies are all placed in the bathroom. For me, who is a little germy, the water and paper towels placed in the bathroom are used for washing and wiping hands, which is very inconvenient. 5. Finally, let‚Äôs talk about the TV. The TV can be stretched, which is undoubtedly very user-friendly. However, most of the TV channels inside are very unclear, and the battery of the remote control is easy to loosen, and it will not work after a while. You have to check it constantly. Check whether the remote control battery is loose.
Not to mention other things, the service, facilities and design of this hotel are really inhumane. The phone number is not clear, the facilities are old, and the design is weird. I really feel lonely here. I should stay here again when I come to Guangzhou in the future. Wouldn't consider staying here again.
